<s> it took her mind off the slowly approaching rite which would give her a freedom but doubtfully desired took her mind too off her boy and his fast approaching departure for a war from which the news remained disquieting <\s>
<s> like bees busy on summer flowers or bright gadflies hovering and darting over spiky autumn blossoms she and her little daughter tall nearly as herself and with a bust measurement not far inferior hovered in the shops of regent street the establishments of hanover square and of bond street lost in consideration and the feel of fabrics <\s>
<s> dozens of young women of striking deportment and peculiar gait paraded before winifred and imogen draped in creations <\s>
<s> the models 'very new modom quite the latest thing which those two reluctantly turned down would have filled a museum the models which they were obliged to have nearly emptied james bank <\s>
<s> it was no good doing things by halves winifred felt in view of the need for making this first and sole untarnished season a conspicuous success <\s>
<s> their patience in trying the patience of those impersonal creatures who swam about before them could alone have been displayed by such as were moved by faith <\s>
<s> it was for winifred a long prostration before her dear goddess fashion fervent as a catholic might make before the virgin for imogen an experience by no means too unpleasant she often looked so nice and flattery was implicit everywhere in a word it was amusing <\s>

<s> imogen's frocks for her first season exercised the judgment of her mother and the purse of her grandfather all through the month of march <\s>
<s> with forsyte tenacity winifred quested for perfection <\s>
<s> it took her mind off the slowly approaching rite which would give her a freedom but doubtfully desired took her mind too off her boy and his fast approaching departure for a war from which the news remained disquieting <\s>
<s> like bees busy on summer flowers or bright gadflies hovering and darting over spiky autumn blossoms she and her little daughter tall nearly as herself and with a bust measurement not far inferior hovered in the shops of regent street the establishments of hanover square and of bond street lost in consideration and the feel of fabrics <\s>
<s> dozens of young women of striking deportment and peculiar gait paraded before winifred and imogen draped in creations <\s>
<s> the models 'very new modom quite the latest thing which those two reluctantly turned down would have filled a museum the models which they were obliged to have nearly emptied james bank <\s>
<s> it was no good doing things by halves winifred felt in view of the need for making this first and sole untarnished season a conspicuous success <\s>
<s> their patience in trying the patience of those impersonal creatures who swam about before them could alone have been displayed by such as were moved by faith <\s>
<s> it was for winifred a long prostration before her dear goddess fashion fervent as a catholic might make before the virgin for imogen an experience by no means too unpleasant she often looked so nice and flattery was implicit everywhere in a word it was amusing <\s>
<s> on the afternoon of the 20th of march having as it were gutted skywards they had sought refreshment over the way at caramel and baker's and stored with chocolate frothed at the top with cream turned homewards through berkeley square of an evening touched with spring <\s>
<s> opening the door freshly painted a light olive green nothing neglected that year to give imogen a good send off winifred passed towards the silver basket to see if anyone had called and suddenly her nostrils twitched <\s>
<s> what was that scent <\s>
<s> imogen had taken up a novel sent from the library and stood absorbed <\s>
<s> rather sharply because of the queer feeling in her breast winifred said take that up dear and have a rest before dinner <\s>
<s> imogen still reading passed up the stairs <\s>
<s> winifred heard the door of her room slammed to and drew a long savouring breath <\s>
<s> was it spring tickling her senses whipping up nostalgia for her clown against all wisdom and outraged virtue <\s>
<s> a faint reek of cigars and lavender water not smelt since that early autumn night six months ago when she had called him the limit <\s>
<s> whence came it or was it ghost of scent sheer emanation from memory <\s>
<s> she looked round her <\s>
<s> nothing not a thing no tiniest disturbance of her hall nor of the diningroom <\s>
<s> a little day dream of a scent illusory saddening silly <\s>

<s> polegate thom and one with mr <\s>
<s> polegate thom thereon she sniffed them but they smelled severe <\s>
<s> i must be tired she thought i'll go and lie down <\s>
<s> upstairs the drawing room was darkened waiting for some hand to give it evening light and she passed on up to her bedroom <\s>
<s> this too was half curtained and dim for it was six o'clock <\s>
<s> winifred threw off her coat that scent again then stood as if shot transfixed against the bed rail <\s>
<s> something dark had risen from the sofa in the far corner <\s>
<s> a word of horror in her family escaped her god <\s>

<s> you have asked her you know murmured jolyon <\s>
<s> the idea was new to her then it came as a shock <\s>
<s> but the more she thinks of it the more she must see that it's the only way out for both of us <\s>
<s> that's not my impression of her state of mind said jolyon with particular calm <\s>
<s> and forgive my saying you misconceive the matter if you think reason comes into it at all <\s>
<s> he saw his cousin's pale face grow paler he had used without knowing it irene's own words <\s>
<s> thanks muttered soames but i see things perhaps more plainly than you think <\s>
<s> i only want to be sure that you won't try to influence her against me <\s>
<s> i don't know what makes you think i have any influence said jolyon but if i have i'm bound to use it in the direction of what i think is her happiness <\s>
<s> i am what they call a feminist i believe <\s>
<s> repeated soames as if seeking to gain time <\s>
<s> does that mean that you're against me <\s>
<s> bluntly said jolyon i'm against any woman living with any man whom she definitely dislikes <\s>
<s> it appears to me rotten <\s>
<s> and i suppose each time you see her you put your opinions into her mind <\s>
<s> i am not likely to be seeing her <\s>

<s> well that's all i had to say <\s>

<s> parsons would have it that freedom of soul and body were quite different things <\s>
<s> body and soul could not thus be separated <\s>
<s> free will was the strength of any tie and not its weakness <\s>

<s> but he's tragic too <\s>
<s> was there anything indeed more tragic in the world than a man enslaved by his own possessive instinct who couldn't see the sky for it or even enter fully into what another person felt <\s>

<s> he had got nothing out of that disingenuous question <\s>

<s> i have some breathing space he's not going back to paris unless he was lying <\s>
<s> i'll let the spring come <\s>
<s> though how the spring could serve him save by adding to his ache he could not tell <\s>
